# File: monster.txt

# This file is used to initialize the "lib/data/monster.raw" file,
# which is used to initialize the "monster race" information for the
# Angband game.

# Do not modify this file unless you know exactly what you are doing,
# unless you wish to risk possible system crashes and broken savefiles.
# After modifying this file, delete the "lib/data/monster.raw" file.

# See "lib/docs/modding.rtf" to understand this file and how to modify
# it and related files.

# Monster.txt entry format

# N: serial number : monster name
# G: symbol : color
# I: speed : hit points : vision : armor class : alertness
# W: depth : rarity : group index : experience for kill
# Autogenerated:
#   C: calculated depth : rarity : group index : calculated experience for kill at the calculated depth : calculated experience for kill at the 'W' depth
# M: innate frequency : spell frequency : spell power : mana
# B: attack method : attack effect : damage
# S: spell type | spell type | etc
# F: flag | flag | etc
# D: Description

# Version stamp (required)


V:0.6.6
